 unhone kaha ki bangla film main kaam karnaa ghar vaapasi karne jaisaa he
 Sushmita (38) said on Sunday on the occasion of the launch of a showroom of jewelery, 'I am going to Kolkata after four days i am very excited to shoot my first Bengali film
 yah mere liye ghar vaapasi jaisaa he, apni jadon main lautne jaisaa he
 See in pictures the cool life of Sushmita Sen
 She told that earlier she was nervous about working in Bengali films, but now she has no fear
 unhone kaha, 'main tamil film main kaam kar sakati hum, telugu film main kaam kar sakati hum, lekin bangla film main kaam karne se dar lagata tha
 It is not so now
 main behtareen abhinaytaon ke saath kaam kar rahi hum or behad utsahit hum
 See, Sushmita Sen's unseen picture is directed by National Award winning director Shreejit Mukherjee
 venkatesh films ke binar tale ban rahi film main jissu sengupta or ruthvik chakravarti bhi honge
 India's richest person Mukesh Ambani is also moving in the list of world's billionaires
 forbs kii duniya ke arbapatiyon kii suchi main vah chah paaydaan kii chalaang lagaakar 13wein sthaan par pahunch gayi hai
 Jeff Bezos, however, continues to occupy the first place on the list

 They are followed by Bill Gates and Warren Buffett
